## <a name="onedrive-for-business-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1930">Recursos do OneDrive for Business</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1930">OneDrive for Business features</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1931"><a name="OfcOnline"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1931"></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1932">O OneDrive for Business (anteriormente SkyDrive pro) é um espaço de armazenamento online pessoal na nuvem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1932">OneDrive for Business (formerly SkyDrive Pro) is personal online storage space in the cloud.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1933">Use-o para armazenar seus arquivos de trabalho em vários dispositivos com facilidade e segurança.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1933">Use it to store your work files across multiple devices with ease and security.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1934">Compartilhe seus arquivos com colegas, conforme necessário, e edite documentos do Office juntos em tempo real com o Office para a Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1934">Share your files with colleagues as needed, and edit Office documents together in real time with Office for the web.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1935">Sincronizar arquivos com o computador local usando o aplicativo de sincronização do OneDrive for Business.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1935">Sync files to your local computer using the OneDrive for Business sync app.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1936">O OneDrive for Business está incluído no SharePoint Online e também pode ser adquirido como um plano independente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1936">OneDrive for Business is included in SharePoint Online and can also be purchased as a standalone plan.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1937">A opção independente do OneDrive for Business inclui o Office para a Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1937">The OneDrive for Business standalone option includes Office for the web.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1938">Para saber mais, confira [o que é o onedrive for Business?](https://support.office.com/article/what-is-onedrive-for-business-187f90af-056f-47c0-9656-cc0ddca7fdc2?ocmsassetID=HA102822076&CorrelationId=fbaf87c5-cecc-42ed-8dca-b40b09b93828&ui=en-US&rs=en-US&ad=US)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1938">To learn more, see [What is OneDrive for Business?](https://support.office.com/article/what-is-onedrive-for-business-187f90af-056f-47c0-9656-cc0ddca7fdc2?ocmsassetID=HA102822076&CorrelationId=fbaf87c5-cecc-42ed-8dca-b40b09b93828&ui=en-US&rs=en-US&ad=US)</span></span>
  
### <a name="system-requirements"></a><span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1939">Requisitos do sistema</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1939">System Requirements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1940">O cliente de sincronização do OneDrive for Business tem requisitos de sistema diferentes dos do cliente OneDrive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1940">The OneDrive for Business sync client has different system requirements than the OneDrive client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1941">Para saber mais, confira [como instalar o cliente de sincronização do onedrive for Business](https://support2.microsoft.com/kb/2903984).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1941">To learn more, see [How to install the OneDrive for Business sync client](https://support2.microsoft.com/kb/2903984).</span></span>
  
### <a name="onedrive-for-business-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1942">Limites do OneDrive for Business</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1942">OneDrive for Business limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1943">O OneDrive for Business plano 1 fornece 1 TB de espaço de armazenamento por usuário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1943">OneDrive for Business Plan 1 provides 1 TB of storage space per user.</span></span> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1944">Os seguintes planos de qualificação oferecem armazenamento ilimitado do OneDrive por usuário para assinaturas com pelo menos cinco usuários.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1944">The following qualifying plans provide unlimited OneDrive storage per user for subscriptions with at least five users.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1945">A Microsoft fornecerá um espaço de armazenamento inicial de 5 TB por usuário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1945">Microsoft will provide an initial 5 TB of storage space per user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1946">Os clientes que desejam armazenamento adicional do OneDrive podem solicitá-lo conforme necessário entrando em contato com o suporte da Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1946">Customers who want additional OneDrive storage can request it as needed by contacting Microsoft Support.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1947">As assinaturas com menos de cinco usuários recebem 1 TB de armazenamento por usuário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1947">Subscriptions with less than five users receive 1 TB of storage per user.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1948">Office 365 A1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1948">Office 365 A1</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1949">Office 365 A3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1949">Office 365 A3</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1950">Office 365 A5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1950">Office 365 A5</span></span>
    
<span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1951">Você não pode alocar mais armazenamento para um usuário específico do OneDrive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1951">You cannot allocate more storage to a specific OneDrive user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1952">No entanto, você pode diminuir a quantidade de armazenamento que um usuário vê.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1952">However, you can lower the amount of storage that a user sees.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1953">Se um usuário do Office 365 Enterprise F1 precisar de mais armazenamento, você precisará atualizar para o Office 365 Enterprise E1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1953">If an Office 365 Enterprise F1 user needs more storage, then you'll need to upgrade to Office 365 Enterprise E1.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1954">Para obter informações sobre tipos de arquivo que você não pode adicionar ao OneDrive for Business, consulte [tipos de arquivos que não podem ser adicionados a uma lista ou biblioteca](https://support.office.com/article/types-of-files-that-cannot-be-added-to-a-list-or-library-30be234d-e551-4c2a-8de8-f8546ffbf5b3?ui=en-US&rs=en-US&ad=US).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1954">For information about file types that you can't add to OneDrive for Business, see [Types of files that cannot be added to a list or library](https://support.office.com/article/types-of-files-that-cannot-be-added-to-a-list-or-library-30be234d-e551-4c2a-8de8-f8546ffbf5b3?ui=en-US&rs=en-US&ad=US).</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1955">O OneDrive for Business vem incluído no SharePoint Online.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1955">OneDrive for Business is included in SharePoint Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-1956">Para saber mais sobre limitações adicionais no SharePoint Online, como cotas de conjunto de sites, limites de carregamento de arquivos e limites de armazenamento, confira limites [e limites de software do SharePoint Online](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/servicedescriptions/sharepoint-online-service-description/sharepoint-online-limits?redirectSourcePath=%252fArticle%252f8f34ff47-b749-408b-abc0-b605e1f6d498).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-1956">To learn about additional limitations in SharePoint Online, such as site collection quotas, file upload limits, and storage limits, see [SharePoint Online software boundaries and limits](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/servicedescriptions/sharepoint-online-service-description/sharepoint-online-limits?redirectSourcePath=%252fArticle%252f8f34ff47-b749-408b-abc0-b605e1f6d498).</span></span>

## <a name="skype-for-business-online-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="a5e66-2958">Recursos do Skype for Business Online</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-2958">Skype for Business Online features</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="a5e66-2959"><a name="OfcOnline"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-2959"></span></span>

### <a name="skype-for-business-online-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="a5e66-3473">Limites do Skype for Business Online</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-3473">Skype for Business Online limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a5e66-3474">Os limites no Skype for Business online caem nas seguintes categorias:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-3474">The limits in Skype for Business Online fall into the following categories:</span></span>
  
- [<span data-ttu-id="a5e66-3475">Limites ponto a ponto</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-3475">Peer-to-peer limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#peer-to-peer-limits)
    
- [<span data-ttu-id="a5e66-3476">Limites de reuniões</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-3476">Meeting limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#meeting-limits)
    
- [<span data-ttu-id="a5e66-3477">Limites de retenção de reunião</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-3477">Meeting retention limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#meeting-retention-limits)
    
- [<span data-ttu-id="a5e66-3478">Limites de minutos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-3478">Minute limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#minute-limits)
    
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-p219">Os limites aplicados a uma organização do Office 365 podem variar, dependendo do tempo pelo qual a organização já está registrada no serviço. Quando um limite é alterado nos datacenters da Microsoft, pode demorar algum tempo para que a alteração seja aplicada a todos os clientes existentes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-p219">The limits applied to an Office 365 organization can differ depending on how long the organization has been enrolled in the service. When a limit is changed in the Microsoft data centers, it can take some time to apply the change to all existing customers.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="peer-to-peer-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="a5e66-3481">Limites ponto a ponto</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-3481">Peer-to-peer limits</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-p220">**Limite de transferência de arquivo** O tamanho máximo de um arquivo que pode ser transferido em uma conversa de IM do Skype for Business online. Para saber quais tipos de arquivos não podem ser transferidos, confira o artigo da Suporte da Microsoft sobre [como enviar e receber arquivos ou anexos no Skype for Business Online](https://support.microsoft.com/help/2799505/you-can-t-send-or-receive-files-or-attachments-in-skype-for-business-o).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-p220">**File transfer limit** The maximum size of a file that can be transferred in a Skype for Business Online IM conversation. To learn which file types are blocked for file transfer, see the Microsoft Support article about [sending and receiving files or attachments in Skype for Business Online](https://support.microsoft.com/help/2799505/you-can-t-send-or-receive-files-or-attachments-in-skype-for-business-o).</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-3484">**Limite de conversas abertas com guias** O número máximo de guias de conversas que um usuário do Skype for Business pode ter abertas de uma só vez.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-3484">**Open tabbed conversations limit** The maximum number of conversation tabs that a Skype for Business user can have open at one time.</span></span>

The full participant list remains visible to the presenters in the meeting. Also, Gallery View and IM errors are hidden from the attendees.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="meeting-retention-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="a5e66-3539">Limites de retenção de reunião</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-3539">Meeting retention limits</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-3540">**Período de retenção de conteúdo de reunião** A quantidade de tempo depois da última pessoa sair de uma reunião em que conteúdos da reunião carregados são retidos no Skype for Business antes de serem excluídos permanentemente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-3540">**Meeting content retention period** The amount of time after the last person leaves a meeting that any uploaded meeting content is retained in Skype for Business before it is permanently deleted.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-3541">**Período de expiração da reunião** A quantidade de tempo durante a qual os usuários podem acessar a reunião após o término da reunião.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-3541">**Meeting expiration period** The amount of time after a meeting has ended that users can access the meeting.</span></span> 
    
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="a5e66-3542">Cada pessoa pode ter no máximo 1000 conferências no banco de dados a qualquer momento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5e66-3542">Each person can have a maximum of 1000 conferences in the database at any time.</span></span>
